Nippur sources more closely resembles that of NP1 than that of NI1. While not a single source

same order as NP1. Moreover sources NI13 and NI14 begin with lines 124 and 129 (of Zgoll's
numbering) and end wiF Fe lines 125 and 125a. We also see no clear reason for not assigning

separate.

follow the line ordering of source NIII22, since it has the most completely preserved list.
